	   1 refactor: Switch to "None" template with Express server
	   2
	   3 This commit refactors the application to remove the Webpack template and its associated dependencies. The goal is to
		 simplify the architecture into a lightweight Electron background process that serves the front-end via a self-contained
		 Express web server.
	   4
	   5 - Removed all Webpack-related configurations and loader packages.
	   6 - Reconfigured forge.config.js to remove the webpack plugin.
	   7 - Re-implemented the main process (main.js) to launch an Express server that hosts static front-end files.
	   8 - Updated package.json to reflect the new, simpler dependency tree and bumped the version to 1.1.0.
